TOP 32 DECKLISTS
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on March 6, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











There is more to this event than just the Top 8. Below are the decklists of the players who finished in 9th through 32nd place. All of them were at most one match win and/or a tiebreaker boost away from the Top 8.
